<div class="freeStarFragrantica" align="center" data-freestar-ad="__300x300" id="fragranticacom_perfume_incontent_1" v-pre>
</div></div></div><div class="grid-x grid-margin-x grid-margin-y"><div class="cell small-6"><likes-rating :perfume_id="14669" chart="show" type-chart="small-chart" colors="retro"></likes-rating></div><div class="cell small-6"><seasons-rating :perfume_id="14669" chart="show" type-chart="small-chart" colors="retro"></seasons-rating></div><div class="small-12 medium-6 text-center" style="max-height: 50px"><div itemprop="aggregateRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/AggregateRating" itemscope><p class="info-note">Perfume rating&nbsp;<span itemprop="ratingValue">4.34</span>&nbsp;out of&nbsp;<span itemprop="bestRating">5</span> with&nbsp;<span itemprop="ratingCount" content="10409">10,409</span> votes<meta itemprop="reviewCount" content="1362"/></p></div></div></div><div class="grid-x grid-margin-x grid-margin-y"><div class="cell small-12" itemprop="description" v-pre><p><b>Allure Homme Sport Eau Extreme</b> by <b>Chanel</b> is a Woody Aromatic fragrance for men. <b>Allure Homme Sport Eau Extreme</b> was launched in 2012. The nose behind this fragrance is Jacques Polge. Top notes are Mandarin Orange, Mint, Cypress and Sage; middle note is Pepper; base notes are Tonka Bean, Musk, Sandalwood and Cedar. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Chanel is launching men's fragrance Chanel Allure Homme Sport Eau
Extreme and adds it to the well-known collection Allure Homme. The
first perfume of this line was launched back in 1999, and several
other versions splashed the market afterwards - Allure Homme Eau
Fraichissante Pour l`Ete, Allure Homme Edition Blanche, Allure Homme
Sport and Allure Homme Sport Cologne Sport.</p>

<p>
Creator of the new Chanel edition is perfumer creator  Jacques Polge
who provided this characteristic combination made of musky shades,
tart spices, aromatic freshness and masculine, woody accords. Sicilian
mandarin, mint, cypress and clary sage are in charge of cold, herbal
refreshment. Tart not of the fragrance is provided by a fine dose of
black pepper, and woody masculine accords consist of cedar and
sandalwood from New Caledonia, shaped and softened by sensual musk and
warm tonka beans. This extreme composition is reflected in a
combination of freshness, tartness, sensuality, sharpness and
strength!
</p>

<p>
Flacon of the new edition has the same shape as previous Chanel Allure
Homme edition in dark color with a silver color ring on the stopper
with engraved name of the brand. Red and white letters on dark body of
the flacon provide dynamics to the edition. The fragrance is available
as 50 and 100ml Eau Extreme.</p>

<p>
Face of the advertising campaign is professional surfer Danny Fully,
while advertising video clips were directed (Chanel presented them in
several versions of advertising clips) by Oscar winner Kathryn
Bigalow.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other languages: <a padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2337754" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Panagiotes"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2309292"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Panagiotes" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2337754ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2337754" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2309292">Panagiotes</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-04"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1730742422" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>One of the few fragrances created in the last 15 years that i can consider to be a masterpiece. A true compliment getter! Chanel never disappoints me, this is no exception. I detect some mint, something else, equally fresh, tonka beans and sandalwood. I can't speak about musk, but there is a vanilla effect, especially in the drydown. An honour to have in my collection, by the way. <br />
<br />
Despite having the name "Sport", i think it is not a summer scent at all! I wear it during fall, winter and the entire spring! Preferably as an office/work scent, but i could go for a beer while wearing this, who really cares? Great compliment getter, as mentioned before! <br />
<br />
For a calming effect, i only spray once behind each ear! If i wanna smell incredibly strong, i spray twice behind each ear, but from a distance, i am afraid of my clothes, as i never spray them with cologne...Anyway, i consistently get 8 hours of longevity, while there is perfect sillage and projection for the first 2.5 hours!<br />
<br />
My heart said "YES"!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="2337754"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=2337754#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2336553" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2336553" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ScottyFrags"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2307627"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2307627.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="ScottyFrags" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2336553ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2336553" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2307627">ScottyFrags</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-03"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1730643304" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Honestly, one of the best, if not THE best sports fragrances for Men out there. Its strong, masculine and fresh. Massive compliment getter from the ladies and never fails to make an impression anytime i wear it. One of my all time favourite fragrances and I'm always running out of bottles.<br />
9/10 for me overall.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="2336553"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=2336553#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2333690" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2333690" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="pvura"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2081048"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="pvura" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2333690ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2333690" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2081048">pvura</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-31">10/31/24 11:34</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>arguably my favorite fragrance i own<br />
<br />
opens up with a nice blend of citrus and mint. the citrus is creamy and smooth as opposed to tart, juicy, or acidic. after about 25 minutes, the fragrance transitions into a very creamy, silky, smooth tonka and woody scent. the slight mintiness and aromatic touch do stick around throughout the life of the fragrance. if i could describe this fragrance in one word, it would be smooth. it never comes across as harsh or abrasive. just beautifully blended.<br />
<br />
this is an absolutely perfect daily wear cologne. i am a university student so i spend most of my day in big lecture halls sitting very close to hundreds of students. i almost never want to wear a nuclear fragrance thats gonna distract other students. the projection on this one is perfect. strong enough to get a compliment from those sitting next to u but not loud enough to choke people out. many people complain about the longevity. however, i would say i get above average longevity on my skin (roughly 7 hours with 3-4 sprays). thats exactly what i want in an everyday fragrance, long lasting with moderate but consistent projection. also, this fragrance lasts a long time on clothes.<br />
<br />
people like to use the phrase "year round fragrance" as a throwaway term. but this is one fragrance i own that i genuinely believe is so versatile you can wear it in all seasons and occasions. fresh, aromatic, and minty for the warmer weather but also sweet and woody for the colder weather. ive never worn this fragrance and felt out of place or uncomfortable. a true masterpiece.<br />
<br />
its also a very good compliment getter. its not the most unique smell in the world but its a scent profile that everyone enjoys. fresh, slightly sweet, and smooth. every time my friends come in for a hug, they always tell me i smell great. <br />
<br />
my only complaint with this fragrance would be that it is so expensive. if it was more affordable (or more clones available on the market) it would be easy to recommend to everyone. i will enjoy my bottle as long as it lasts, though.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />
Smells sweet-orangy, fresh, creamy and slightly woody.. I have smelt lots of mandarin orange and black pepper based fragrances and deodorants.. As a result I can identify this particular olfactory combination quite easily.. This mandarin orange and black pepper dominated smell is easily detectable in Chanel Allure Homme Sport Eau Extreme.. However, what sets this perfume apart is the note of tonka beans.. The tonka beans add a sweet, creamy richness to the mandarin orange-black pepper combination which along with the woody notes help this perfume stand out..<br />
<br />
Longevity is around 5 hours if sprayed on skin.. On clothes the smell stays for around 7 or 8 hours.. Projection is confined to about an arm's length radius..<br />
<br />
Ideal for a hot summer day.. I will always have a bottle of this in my collection !!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="2325841"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=2325841#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2323797" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="2321109"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=2321109#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2319617" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2319617" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="EauDeSparta"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2290486"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2290486.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="EauDeSparta" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2319617ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2319617" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2290486">EauDeSparta</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-18">10/18/24 06:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It is a perfect fragrance for everyday use. Its fresh and energetic notes, particularly with citrus and spices, make you feel rejuvenated and vibrant. This perfume can be comfortably chosen for both work and social settings, offering a conventional style that appeals to a wide audience. With its structure suitable for blind buying, it’s ideal for those looking for an instantly likable scent. While its longevity and projection are average, Allure Homme Sport truly offers a pleasant option for those in search of a light and fresh fragrance. Reflecting a dynamic lifestyle, this perfume becomes an indispensable choice for those seeking a signature scent. 8.5/10<br />
<br />
Allure Homme Sport, her gün kullanım için mükemmel bir parfüm. Ferah ve enerjik notaları, özellikle narenciye ve baharatlarla açıldığında, kendinizi taze ve canlı hissettiriyor. Hem işte hem de sosyal ortamlarda rahatlıkla tercih edilebilecek bu parfüm, alışılmış bir tarz sunarak genel beğeniye hitap ediyor. Kör alışa da uygun yapısıyla, anında sevilecek bir koku arayanlar için ideal. Kalıcılığı ve yayılımı ortalama seviyede olsa da, hafif ve ferah bir parfüm arayanlar için Allure Homme Sport gerçekten hoş bir seçenek sunuyor. Dinamik bir yaşam tarzını yansıtan bu parfüm, imza parfüm arayanlar için vazgeçilmez bir tercih haline geliyor. 8.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="2319617"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=2319617#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2317001" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; -------------------------------------------------------<br />
Purchased November 2020<br />
One-dimensional scent agreed.  Wore this for a few weeks, and then I got citronella essential oil all over it on my shelf and I just never touched it again.  Thinking back on this one what a REGRETFUL PURCHASE.  Being an enthusiast such as myself pisses me off when I amass a large amount of sports, fresh, citrus-based scents that are only best in the spring and maybe summer, particularly if none of them are tried and true through the test of the passage of time.  Nothing beats time, we never will.  We're all just lucky to be here every moment of every day and these products magically improve just because we haven't died yet.  I don't understand that, but it's unexplainable and true because time is like magic.  Just wait a while and everything will be vintage but skyrocket in price and we'll all cry when what we're after is unavailable or extinct because we've decided we miss it so much it's worth taking out a mortgage just to have it in our hands one more time and have a glimpse of it only to realise it looks different and feels different.  These things didn't change.<br />
<br />
We did.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="2276822"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=2276822#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2276815" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Had a bottle of this back in 2016, loved it, had moderate to long lasting performance and solid projection.<br />
<br />
Was contemplating grabbing myself another bottle but decided on getting a 2ml sample due to some people saying it barely lasted an hour on them. <br />
<br />
Thank goodness I didn't buy another bottle.. Still smells amazing, but.... this thing does a Houdini on you pretty fast.  <br />
<br />
I know there is always the chance that I got a bad sample, but it's pretty unlikely. I cannot recommend spending money on this. but if you happen to have some cash burning a hole in your pocket and you don't care about performance/projection, go for it.<br />
<br />
It seems like Chanel has become complacent, relying heavily on this and the Bleu de Chanel line for sales. While they are great scents, it’s time for the brand to stop disrespecting its customers by gradually diluting their products, offering less value for money, and start introducing something new.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2137868">EmilZakaryan924</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-28">07/28/24 14:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I went to the Chanel boutique today to try out some of their mens fragrances.<br />
<br />
This is a well blended masterpiece. This is my 2nd favorite fragrance from the Allure Homme line. Starts off minty, citrusy, woody, with a touch of tonka/vanilla in the base. To my nose, this and the original Allure Homme Sport have kind of the same opening. But this smells better than the original. <br />
<br />
Lets talk about performance. I got around 6-7 hours on my skin with a medium projection leaning on the masculine side. I recommend this fragrance for the spring, summer and maybe the fall. You could wear this in the day and in the night. <br />
<br />
Lastly, is it a safe blind buy? Yes. If you love the Allure Homme DNA, you will love this. <br />
<br />
In conclusion: <br />
Scent: 9.5/10<br />
Longevity: 7/10<br />
Projection: 6.5/10<br />
<br />
Chanel Allure Homme Sport Eau Extreme: 8.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="2232057"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=2232057#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2231935" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; overall the notes of orange are noticeable, but performance flatlines and plateaus at the 3-4 hour mark as with any fresh fragrance do not expect this to last more than 8 hours of wear. <br />
<br />
Scent is mass appealing and likeable, as with any fragrance from the house of Chanel expect a great fragrance but at high price.<br />
<br />
although the opening, you get a blast of fresh citrus the dry down for me can get a bit too cloying. <br />
8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="2207005"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=2207005#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2206825" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Obviously it is higher quality than Versace Eros, but if you want a similar smell that performs far better and is 1/4 of the price on discounters, I’d go with Eros here. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1370156">Afc_Croatian</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-06">06/06/24 06:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>All of my expectations up to buying this fragrance was that it would be a fresh minty sport fragrance with considerable longevity.<br />
... I have never been more surprised by a fragrance.<br />
<br />
First of all, I swear there is a star anise note in this scent (very subtle licorice), reading the notes list I can't tell what note would give off that vibe. That note alone threw me off, I was expecting a summer freshie, this is another example of how Chanel knows how to make versatile scents that just blow me away.<br />
<br />
Next, I am pleased with its performance, much longer performance than its flankers IMO and that bold note lingers for hours for me. The dry down is solid, I enjoy a smooth tonka any day of the week. That orange notes disappears quick and those heavy notes overpower it almost immediately.<br />
<br />
Chanel did a great job with adding just enough mint cypress and orange to make it a summer scent but IMO it's more of a date night fragrance for me.<br />
<br />
8.5/10 Chanel you have done it again.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="2179883"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=2179883#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2178151" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

After it dries down, the tonka bean becomes the main note in this fragrance, being nicely balanced out by the perfect amount of mandarin orange and an almost lemon rind smell. <br />
An amazingly blended fragrance, as are most of Chanel's.<br />
8/10 from me, good for hot summer days, but performance isn't the greatest.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="2144299"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=2144299#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2142116" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; AHS is for the players, AHSE is for the coach oh yeah.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="2118628"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=2118628#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2118553" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2048988">Oldchief61</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-18">03/18/24 13:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Chanel fragrances have never failed to yield good returns on my investments in quality, performance, and longevity; Allure Homme Sport Eau Extrême is no exception. When I wear Parfum strength fragrances the likes of Krigler, Creed, Amouage, Bond No.9, et.al., I become anosmic (nose blind) to the scent within an hour. I can't smell it, but others still can. When I read comments about poor performance and longevity for Eau de Parfum/Parfum fragrances, I can't help but conjure the mental image of some anosmic individual over-applying this fragrance then going out, sniffing his arm, while trees and foliage wither and birds fall out of the sky around him. As with all fragrances, their performance depends on your body chemistry, skin moisture, overall health, diet, your mood, medications, and climate. <br />
<br />
Allure Homme Sport Eau Extrême is a fragrance that radiates a well-blended balance of youthful vigor and mature refinement for a solid 6-7 hours. Mint, Pepper, and Cypress evoke youthful energy, Tonka, Musk, and Sandalwood emit a sophisticated warmth anchored in maturity. Allure Homme Sport Eau Extrême is not just a scent; it pays homage to the active, modern man who values dynamic and understated sophistication. The scent isn't bold and loud; it sneaks up on you. Chanel has, yet again, crafted a scent that is a harmonious marriage of the athletic and the elegant, making Allure Homme Sport Eau Extrême a standard accessory for the contemporary, masculine male.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; The bottle represents the juice well I believe. It has a kind of silver vibe to it, almost futuristic imo.<br />
<br />
Citrusy opening to a high quality creamy powdery tonka dry down, with some mint adding freshness. <br />
Anyways, I love it. So smooth. For me the performance is moderate. 2018 batch.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="2073720"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=2073720#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2071660" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2063170" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ninjandrew"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1642457"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1642457.gif" class="comments-avatar"alt="ninjandrew" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/DS-Durga/Bowmakers-22058.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.22058.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Bowmakers"title="Bowmakers"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2063170ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2063170" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1642457">ninjandrew</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-15">02/15/24 10:18</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A quick review as a comparison between this and regular Allure Homme Sport.<br />
<br />
Eau extreme opens with more citrus than the regular, and with a bit of mint. The mint is the first to go, and orange lasts for a few hours before being replaced by tonka bean and sandalwood. <br />
<br />
Regular Allure Homme Sport also has a citrusy opening but shares this space with strong marine notes, aldehydes and vanilla. The marine notes last for a few hours slowly giving up to more vanilla and tonka bean.<br />
<br />
While I would consider both of these fragrances to belong to the sport category, I find them both a bit on the creamy side and so aren't the sportiest frags out there, though they could have their place as sporty "cool weather" fragrances. <br />
<br />
From this family, I would recommend Allure Homme Edition Blanche if you want more citrus and less cream.<br />
<br />
Both are pleasant and with good performance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="2063170"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=2063170#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2060024" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2060024" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Djchildress"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1219467"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1219467.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Djchildress" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Afnan/Supremacy-Not-Only-Intense-68271.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.68271.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Supremacy Not Only Intense"title="Supremacy Not Only Intense"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2060024ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2060024" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1219467">Djchildress</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-12">02/12/24 09:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The cypress, sage and mandarin in the opening of this fragrance are exquisitely done!!! I find it rare for me to really be drawn in by a very well done cypress note, but when I do run across one such as in this, Banana Republics Cypress and Cedar, and most definitely the way it's portrayed in Thameen's Carved Oud, I just can't get enough of it. I even really enjoyed the way that note was done in Invictus Platinum by Paco Rabanne. The way it rounds out the citrus top notes and makes them come across so much more juicy than they would without the green accord lending them an added zest. With the current wave of green fragrances coming out I'm definitely looking forward to more in this general direction with a little sweetness, good longevity, bright, juicy citruses and a good amberwood/ambroxan base but with more contrast that what we've had with the run of the mill blue frags. Allure Homme Eau Extreme is probably the best year round office friendly fragrance I can think of for younger men, but I still have it in my rotation regularly despite many niche and indie fragrances in my collection. It just works, and it does everything so well that it's hard to dislike this one.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="2060024"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=2060024#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2059774" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2059774" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Docrj"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1891275"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Docrj" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2059774ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2059774" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1891275">Docrj</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-12">02/12/24 03:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This here is a masterpiece. Opening is not its strong point but the mid and dry down is heavenly. I sprayed this on both forearms last night to test its longevity. I was disappointed because when i woke up about 6hrs later it was already a faint skin scent. So I made breakfast and ate at the kitchen and when I got back to my room... Man, the room still smells like CAHSEE! This sillage of this thing is amazing! So I figured people who wear this easily get nose blinded and label it as a poor performer. I also have a Versace Pour Homme which everybody says smells very similar to this one. But to my nose, CAHSEE smells more citrusy, smooth and powdery than the Versace. I even compared this to the Missoni Wave which others say also smells similar to the Chanel. But to my nose, they only smell about 70% similar in the opening. In the dry down, the Chanel is miles better in scent quality and smoothness. <br />
<br />
I have the 08/2023 batch and this one performs exceptionally well in my opinion. I really do think this perfume should form part of every fragrance lover's collection. Definitely a 10/10 for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="2059774"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=2059774#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2059126" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; And Eau Extreme is the best of the line. <br />
People complaining about high prices - yes, fragrances are high price luxury items. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2046228" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Smellybutgood"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1593587"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1593587.gif" class="comments-avatar"alt="Smellybutgood" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Hermes/Terre-d-Hermes-17.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.17.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Terre d'Hermès"title="Terre d'Hermès"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2046228ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2046228" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1593587">Smellybutgood</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-29">01/29/24 19:23</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This fragrance is a delightful choice for spring and summertime but is versatile enough for cooler weather as well. It epitomizes a classic fougère, tailored for the carefree individual seeking a clean, fresh, and masculine scent.<br />
<br />
History if you're interested. <br />
<br />
The Allure Homme series made its debut in 1999, marking Chanel's first venture into men's fragrances. Since then, it has expanded with four notable flankers: <br />
(Blanche EDT and EDP are the same fragrance,  just a label change i.e. marketing)<br />
<br />
1. **Allure Homme Sport** – launched in 2004<br />
2. **Allure Homme Sport Cologne** – introduced in 2007<br />
3. **Allure Homme Edition Blanche EDT** – released in 2008<br />
4. **Allure Homme Sport Eau Extreme** – unveiled in 2012.<br />
5. **Allure Homme Edition Blanche EDP** – released in 2014<br />
<br />
The fragrance landscape changed with the introduction of Allure Homme Sport Cologne in response to the need for a summer scent. Laden with citrus and fresh spices, its performance and longevity fell short of expectations. In a bid to address this, Chanel swiftly launched Allure Homme Edition Blanche 2008 just one year after the Sport Cologne. <br />
<br />
Four years later, Allure Homme Sport Extreme hit the market, earning acclaim for its exceptional performance and fragrance, making it a standout among the Allure collection. Personally, it tops my list, closely followed by the original 1999 Allure and Blanche after.<br />
<br />
Given its broad appeal and penchant for garnering compliments, Chanel Allure Homme Sport Eau Extreme stands out, despite its relatively higher price point. While it may be considered a bit of a splurge, it undeniably offers a premium experience.<br />
<br />
Hint, Hint! To the average nose, distinguishing between Eau Extreme, Missoni Wave, or Versace Pour Homme might prove challenging. 🤫</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="2046228"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=2046228#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2037283" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2020562" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Psalzarulo"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1723203"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Psalzarulo" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2020562ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2020562" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1723203">Psalzarulo</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-04">01/04/24 18:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I've owned this scent for years but am just getting around to reviewing it. <br />
<br />
This is honestly an amazing scent and deserves its high status. Being a Chanel scent, it's very classy and subdued. However, the combination of citrus, musk, and mild aromatics make this a dark, seductive scent. The dry-down, to me, retains the sweet, musky orange notes and last for at least 6 hours. <br />
<br />
As an aside, I smelled the regular Allure Home and hated it.<br />
<br />
This definitely leans more mature, but is wearable in nearly any weather, setting and occasion. I do occasionally wear it to work, but I do try and save it for special occasions as I have other scents I use for everyday use. I've found it's a very good compliment-getter. <br />
<br />
I really think the key to this scent is the subtlety and simplify of the citrusy musk. It may not be something you smell once and are immediately impressed by, but I think once you wear it and experience it, you'll get the hype. <br />
<br />
I think this is a rare 10/10 for me. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1656862">dokei</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-06">11/06/23 13:37</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This opens lightly for about 1 min and then an overpowering cinnamon and spices take this to almost gourmand levels. Sandalwood is present but id say its quite synthetic. I dont get the opening notes at all other than a the mint for the first minute.<br />
It does last about 3h on my skin but that is actually good, for comparison sauvage elixir lasts about 6h (i have sand for skin and most perfumes dont last 3+h).<br />
Sillage is medium, which is good, it makes this versatile and private.<br />
Scent profile is definitely on the sweet side for me. but this is a good daily no problem. Not for super hot days as it might choke people out.<br />
<br />
70eur for 50ml and for that price id say this is worth it for people who like this kind of fragrance. Not a safe blind buy though, but if you see it under 50eur for 50ml go for it, you will end up reaching to put it on.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="1970206"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=1970206#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1969526" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1969526" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="jj7642"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1703776"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1703776.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="jj7642" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Mancera/Cedrat-Boise-15211.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.15211.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Cedrat Boise"title="Cedrat Boise"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1969526ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1969526" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1703776">jj7642</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-05">11/05/23 18:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Well, I have to go ahead and eat crow.  I once wrote a review describing this as a mass appealing, generic, and basic fragrance.  However, after putting a sizeable decant through it's paces... oh how wrong I was.  This may be the single smoothest, most well blended fragrance ever.  Plus, the performance is just right - long lasting, never overpowering, but very noticeable.  The versatility is off the charts - there is literally no situation this fragrance doesn't excel.  Now I will say it is a bit expensive - but IMO this is one of the few cases where the quality justifies the price tag.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="1969526"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=1969526#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1968880" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1968880" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Dontknowaname"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1883263"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1883263.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Dontknowaname" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Xerjoff/Erba-Pura-55157.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.55157.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Erba Pura"title="Erba Pura"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1968880ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1968880" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1883263">Dontknowaname</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-04">11/04/23 21:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>If I had to explain this fragrance with only two words, those words would be Tonka Explosion. As soon as you put this one on, you are blasted with slight freshness, citrus, and musk along with the dominant sweet but not medicinal tonka bean. It is the best interpretation of tonka bean I have ever smelled as of yet, far better than that of Le Beau and Le Male Elixir of JPG. The tonka stays mostly dominant throughout the lifespan, with different scents sprinkled perfectly in balance with a sporty but jack of all trades type of fragrance. First, you get the orange. Juicy while not being overly citrusy, unlike that of the lemon in Edition Blanche. As the fragrance develops, you start to get some spice from the pepper. It is not overwhelmingly spicy but is noticeable and goes perfectly with the star of the show. Throughout, you get a white musk. I'd say it is the second most dominant note in the fragrance. It is more prominent at times and softer at others, but it is never screechy or harsh. This fragrance is smooth, extremely elegant and blended to perfection. At the tail end of the lifespan of projection, you get some woods. Most dominantly sandalwood, but you could possibly pick out some cedar although I was not able to. The only complaint about this fragrance, which is not a not a big problem since it can be fixed to an extent, is the performance. It projects for about three hours, and while it is nowhere close to filling a room, it will definitely be pretty easy to pick up on to anyone close to you. The longevity is the main issue for me. It lasts about five pushing six hours. But after the two or three of projection, the only thing I pick up on in the skin scent is the tonka bean of course, and maybe a little musk and sandalwood. Although for the latter two, you really have to look for them to smell them. You can wear this anywhere, anytime except for cold winter days. To put it simply, this is a great sporty fragrance with sweet and sexy freshness with a little bit of warmth. In conclusion, Chanel Allure Homme Sport Eau Extreme is a great fragrance, and is a definite repurchase for me. I think the masterclass of blending, top-notch quality, and sheer elegance justify the expensive price point for this designer fragrance. Also, if you're wondering, this is miles better than the original Chanel Allure Homme Sport. MILES.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="1968880"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=1968880#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1968208" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I’m 18 and I love it just as much as my 43 year old dad.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="1966727"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=1966727#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1955373" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1859983">FriXionZ</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-10-18">10/18/23 15:47</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>After smelling normal allure homme I really liked it and so decided to pick up a bottle of eau extreme at the airport, tax-free so I only paid about 50 euros for a 50ml bottle. <br />
<br />
After trying it on for the first time I noticed it was quite a bit different from the normal AHS, this opening is a little less fresh and already has stronger wood notes coming out, not worse by any means, but different. Dry down is great but also different from OG AHS, again the wood notes are more pronounced here. I was quite disappointed by its performance, decent projection and sillage but only got about 5 hours longevity (4 sprays, batch number 8001) <br />
<br />
I think for a fresh fragrance I would prefer the normal AHS since it's opening is alot more citrussy and aquatic but I like what they did with the wood notes and tonka bean with this one. Use OG AHS for the summer and this for early spring and fall and you have some killer fragrances on your hands.<br />
<br />
If the performance was a little better, easy 9/10 since this DNA smells great from start to finish. Taking performance into account, 7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="1955373"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=1955373#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1953998" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1257875">pshopper1180</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-10-04">10/04/23 08:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>An Athletic Elegance:<br />
<br />
Allure Homme Sport Eau Extrême is a fragrance that radiates a perfect balance of vigor and refinement. From the first spritz, the invigorating freshness of mint catapults you into a realm of endless energy, preparing you for the adventures the day holds. As the scent evolves, the smooth richness of tonka bean emerges, embracing you in a sophisticated warmth that is both comforting and empowering. The subtle earthiness of the base notes grounds this fragrance, portraying a robust character that is unyielding yet welcoming. Its lasting power is admirable, enduring through your most active moments and settling into a gentle, appealing trace that beckons admiration from others. The sillage is a harmonious blend of assertion and subtlety, marking your presence elegantly in any room. Allure Homme Sport Eau Extrême is not just a scent; it's a testament to the active, modern man who values a seamless blend of dynamism and sophistication. Its bottle, sleek with a masculine edge, encapsulates the essence of the fragrance impeccably. Chanel has, yet again, crafted a scent that is a harmonious marriage of the athletic and the elegant, making Allure Homme Sport Eau Extrême a quintessential companion for the contemporary man.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1766190">nirvblakr</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-05">09/05/23 23:18</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>No tester, blind buy because of the hype. Sprayed this on before going to the gym (best to test) because of its marketing as Sport Eau Extreme. Opening is strong with a sweet citrus smell. Sprayer is good that's why just one spray a large surface area is covered. Mid dry down going vanillic and musky then dries down with a  spicy accord. When sprayed in the arm, the spicy smell isn't really flattering. Like the dry down of D&amp;g light Blue Intense - plasticky which makes me dizzy. But it won't be as evident if sprayed at the back which most probably the others won't smell.<br />
Doing the treadmill,  the musky odor is evident but not singled out as it had a plethora of other scents like sweet citrus aromatic that's blending. The more sweat the more smell it emits. I wouldn't be surprised if my smell was cloying to other people near me.<br />
I guess this isn't really made for heavy workouts. For golf maybe.<br />
For everyday use, better for outdoor activities but it can also be worn indoors at work or school. Definitely not for night functions. <br />
Performance wise seemed weak (need to confirm again) considering that it has a musky accord. I guess the freshie citrus accords tamed it down a bit. <br />
Personally, I think it's expensive for the performance and scent. You might just be paying for the Chanel name as it rides with the success of BDC.<br />
I will prefer JPG Ultramale over this which is more reasonably priced.<br />
I got a lot of compliments on resprays. This is from an atomizer where I transferred my frag. I think the transfer from the original bottle to the atomizer worked magic!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="1920835"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=1920835#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1915144" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1825399">RedeemedAndRestored521</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-08-28">08/28/23 19:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>When I smell this I think: <br />
Smooth, masculine, minty, peppery, vanilla-sweet-tonka bean, musk. <br />
Seems to lean more natural compared to the synthetic fragrances out there like Ysl Y, versace pour homme, bleu de chanel, dylan blue, etc... <br />
Not too dense and not cloying at all. <br />
It's not offensive and it is very pleasant when you smell it in the air as you walk by and move around. I personally find this to be very pleasant and I find myself smelling it on my arm here and there throughout the day. I find it to be unique. <br />
If you have the money and it doesn't break the bank, I'd say it's worth it. The drydown in my opinion is very very nice. Slightly similar to that of versace pour homme's drydown (tonka bean + musk) but not even close to being identical. I actually can't think of a fragrance that I can call "close" to this. It is unique. <br />
<br />
Personally,<br />
Scent: 9/10<br />
Longevity, sillage, projection: average. Not beast mode. But not bad at all. <br />
Those who say it's performance is poor have just gone nose blind to it. It's the same people who say that 6 sprays is a normal amount (that will choke people out. Honest people around you will tell you this). Very often, you cannot smell a fragrance on you after a few minutes, but others can. <br />
<br />
It's expensive just like all chanel fragrances. I suggest you test it out before buying.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="1913928"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=1913928#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1903009" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; longevity 9/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="762469"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=762469#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent462630" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc462630" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="heartcooksbrain"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/601062"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.601062.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="heartcooksbrain" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Burberry/London-for-Men-804.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.804.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="London for Men"title="London for Men"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma462630ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd462630" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/601062">heartcooksbrain</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2014-03-02">03/02/14 10:17</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>People can complain about how many flankers Chanel puts out all they want. My honest opinion is that Chanel makes the best flankers out there, and most of them could stand on their own. This "extreme" version of Allure Homme Sport may be portrayed wrong by the title. I will agree the naming of this scent is off, but I'm reviewing the fragrance, not the name. Allure Homme sport is a wonderful fragrance, but on my skin it didn't last as long as I wanted it to, even though it does last longer than most summer fragrances. Eau Extreme is the answer to that problem, atleast for me. It takes the best elements from Allure Homme Sport and adds more tonka bean to give it a more mature, deeper scent. This combination of citrus and heavy tonka is blended wonderfully to create a long lasting scent that will please most if not all who come in contact with it. It's strong enough for the colder months, yet still light enough to wear in the spring/summer. This makes it versatile and well deserving of being a signature scent for someone just to wear all the time. It's perfect for a date night, or wherever you work on a daily basis. I don't get all the criticism, which I'm aware that people have different likes and dislikes when it comes to fragrances, but sometimes I think people expect or demand too much, all while not even knowing what it is they're demanding. This is a great, manly fragrance that will please people. End of story.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="462630"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=462630#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1095897" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/26795">nattonline</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2012-06-04">06/04/12 13:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I have been wearing this for quite some time, and I still don't know what to think of it. For sure, this is nothing like Allure Homme Sport. It's not a lemoney scent anymore.  I get a lot of tonka bean. It's syrupy but not all that sweet. It's rich and rather heavy. Not exactly fresh nor it is totally warm either. Everything smells pleasantly weird to me, especially the mint (or basil?). Not a blind buy and it requires multiple tests before making a final decision. For me, the best way to go is to get a lot of sample or a decant, that's all I'd really need.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="14669"comment_id="256658"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html?ccid=256658#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="14669" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
